STARTUP API documentation version 1.0

http://gateway.api.nextspace.platform.org/

天下拉手platform api gateway接口规范

天下拉手接口规范

语义规范

Get

获取资源的某个表述

post

基于给定的表述信息，在当前资源的下一级创建新的资源

Delete

销毁一个资源

Patch

根据提供的表述信息修改资源的部分状态。如果有某些资源状态在提供的表述中没有被提到， 这些状态就保持不变。类似于Put，但是允许对资源状态进行一些细粒度的改动

/members

会员资源

/members/register post

post

注册会员

post /members/register

注册会员

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberRegister",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员注册",
  "properties": {
    "phone": {
      "description": "手机号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "name": {
      "description": "名称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "roles": {
      "description": "角色",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "verifyCode": {
      "description": "验证码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "verifyCodeType": {
      "description": "验证码类型",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "password": {
      "description": "密码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "imei": {
      "description": "设备号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": true
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberRegisterSuccess",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员注册成功",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "description": "会员id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "phonenum": {
      "description": "手机号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "interestTags": {
      "description": "兴趣标签列表",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "interest-tag"
      }
    },
    "imtoken": {
      "description": "IM token",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 400

参数格式不正确或参数个数不正确

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

OAuth签名不正确

HTTP status code 403

对资源的访问被拒绝。通常这意味着当前请求被限制。也可能是你没有访问此资源的权限

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",

    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",

        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",

        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/login get

get

登录

get /members/login

登录

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • phone: (string)
  • password: (string)
  • imei: (string)

    设备号

  • verifyCode: (string)

HTTP status code 200

登录成功响应

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Member",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "description": "会员id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "nickname": {
      "description": "会员昵称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "headImg": {
      "description": "头像",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "phonenum": {
      "description": "手机号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "password": {
      "description": "登陆密码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "email": {
      "description": "邮箱",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "type": {
      "description": "会员类型",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "birthday": {
      "description": "生日",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "gender": {
      "description": "性别",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "registerTime": {
      "description": "注册时间",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "loginTime": {
      "description": "登陆时间",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "status": {
      "description": "会员状态",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "emailBindStatus": {
      "description": "邮箱绑定状态",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "interested": {
      "description": "会员感兴趣的标签",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "interest-tag"
      }
    },
    "imtoken": {
      "description": "IM token",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 400

参数格式不正确或参数个数不正确

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

{
  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

/members/resetpassword patch

patch

会员重置密码

会员重置密码

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

Type: application/json

Schema:

  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberResetPassword",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员重置密码",
  "properties": {
    "phone": {
      "description": "手机号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "newPassword": {
      "description": "新密码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": true
    },
    "code": {
      "description": "验证码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/verifyimgcode get

get

获取图片验证码的值

get /members/verifyimgcode

获取图片验证码的值

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • phone: (string)

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.VerifyCode",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "验证码",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "description": "id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "code": {
      "description": "验证码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "type": {
      "description": "类型",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "desc": {
      "description": "描述",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 400

参数格式不正确或参数个数不正确

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

{
  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

      "description": "集合",

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id} get

get

查询会员信息

get /members/{member_id}

查询会员信息

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

post /members/{member_id}/interesttags

注册成功，设置兴趣内容

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberInterest",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员兴趣及昵称设置",
  "properties": {
    "memberId": {
      "description": "会员id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "nickname": {
      "description": "昵称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "gender": {
      "description": "性别",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "interested": {
      "description": "会员感兴趣的标签",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "interest-tag"
      }
    }
  }
}

      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

patch /members/{member_id}/profile

修改会员个人信息

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberProfile",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "description": "会员id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "nickname": {
      "description": "会员昵称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "headImg": {
      "description": "头像",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "birthday": {
      "description": "生日",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "gender": {
      "description": "性别",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "interested": {
      "description": "会员感兴趣的标签",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "interest-tag"
      }
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id}/changephone patch

patch

会员修改手机号

patch /members/{member_id}/changephone

会员修改手机号

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberChangePhone",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员重置手机号",
  "properties": {
    "oldPhone": {
      "description": "旧手机号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "newPhone": {
      "description": "新手机号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": true
    }
  }
}

  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

验证邮箱是否可绑定

get /members/{member_id}/email/verify

验证邮箱是否可绑定

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • email: (string)

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  "description": "会员地址列表",
  "properties": {
    "addresses": {
      "description": "地址列表",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "member-address"
      }

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

post /members/{member_id}/addresses

新增地址信息

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberAddress",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员地址信息",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "description": "地址id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "type": {
      "description": "地址类型",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "typeName": {
      "description": "地址类型名称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "image": {
      "description": "地址图标",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "location": {
      "description": "地图定位",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "address": {
      "description": "详细地址",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "isDefault": {
      "description": "是否默认",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "title": {
      "description": "标题",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "contact": {

      "type": "string",
      "required": false

    "phone": {

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

delete /members/{member_id}/addresses/{address_id}

删除地址

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)
  • address_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

/members/{member_id}/credits get

get

查看积分状态

get /members/{member_id}/credits

查看积分状态

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • direction: (string)

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.model.MemberCredits",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "积分列表",
  "properties": {
    "memberId": {
      "description": "用户id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "currentCredits": {
      "description": "当前积分",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "frozenCredits": {
      "description": "冻结积分",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "totalCredits": {
      "description": "总积分",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "credits": {
      "description": "列表",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "member-credit-detail"
      }
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "数量",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id}/credits/linkurl get

get

获取登陆链接

get /members/{member_id}/credits/linkurl

获取登陆链接

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • redirect: (string)

/members/{member_id}/credits/items get

get

查看积分列表

get /members/{member_id}/credits/items

查看积分列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • direction: (string)

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id}/credits/minus post

post

减积分

post /members/{member_id}/credits/minus

减积分

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Schema:

  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

HTTP status code 403

对资源的访问被拒绝。通常这意味着当前请求被限制。也可能是你没有访问此资源的权限

Type: application/json

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id}/scenes get post

场景

get

获取会员的场景列表

post

新增场景

get /members/{member_id}/scenes

获取会员的场景列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • params: (string)

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberScenes",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员的场景集合",
  "properties": {
    "scenes": {
      "description": "集合",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "member-scene"
      }
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "总数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

{
  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

patch /members/{member_id}/scenes/{scene_id}

修改场景信息

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)
  • scene_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-modified-since: (integer - minimum: 0)

    Value as a Unix time stamp of milliseconds since epoch.

    Example:

    1267401600000
  • x-la-modified: (one of updated, create)

    Values are updated or new.

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberScene",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员的场景",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "description": "场景id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "name": {
      "description": "场景名称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "title": {
      "description": "场景名称中文",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "address": {
      "description": "地址",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "picture": {
      "description": "图片地址",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "lat": {
      "description": "纬度",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "lng": {
      "description": "经度",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "sceneType": {
      "description": "场景类型",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "sceneTypeId": {
      "description": "场景类型Id",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "tags": {
      "description": "标签",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

  • item_id: required (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

/members/{member_id}/notifications/management get

get

查看待管理列表

get /members/{member_id}/notifications/management

查看待管理列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MessageManage",
  "description" : "提醒管理",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "added": {
      "description": "已添加",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "message-type"
      }
    },
    "notAdded": {
      "description": "未添加",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "message-type"
      }
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • status: (string)

        "$ref": "order"

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

get

订单状态数字列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • status: (string)

  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false

        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id}/orders/{order_id}/confirmreceived post

post

确认订单收货

post /members/{member_id}/orders/{order_id}/confirmreceived

确认订单收货

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)
  • order_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.MemberOrderConfirmReceived",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "会员订单收货确认",
  "properties": {
    "orderId": {
      "description": "订单ID",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "channel": {
      "description": "渠道",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "channelCode": {
      "description": "渠道码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

请求成功

Type: application/json

Schema:

      "required": false

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/members/{member_id}/orders/{order_id}/refundreason get

get

查询退款原因列表

get /members/{member_id}/orders/{order_id}/refundreason

查询退款原因列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • member_id: required (string)
  • order_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/delegate/scenes/switch/scenetypes get

get

获取场景类型列表

get /delegate/scenes/switch/scenetypes

获取场景类型列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

      "description": "集合",

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/delegate/scenes/switch/recommend get

get

场景推荐

get /delegate/scenes/switch/recommend

场景推荐

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",

        "required": false
    },

        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",

  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/delegate/scenes/datum get

get

获取当前场景数据

get /delegate/scenes/datum

获取当前场景数据

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • requestType: (string)

        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

  • guid: required (string)

/delegate/contents

拉取内容

/delegate/contents/today get

get

获取当日内容列表

get /delegate/contents/today

获取当日内容列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.ContentsStreams",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "内容集合",
  "properties": {
    "stream": {
      "description": "集合",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "contents-stream"
      }
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "总数-所有内容总条数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "totalStreamCount": {
      "description": "内容流总数-按场景",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "contentStrategy": {
      "description": "内容显示策略，0-全量，1-增量",
      "type" : "string",
      "enum" : ["0", "1"],
      "javaEnumNames" : ["ALL", "INCREMENT"]
    },
    "lastTime": {
      "description": "最后内容时间",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "totalHistoryContentCount": {
      "description": "历史内容总数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/delegate/contents/history get

get

获取往期内容列表

get /delegate/contents/history

获取往期内容列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • beforeTime: (string)

    在此时间之前

  • pageNo: (integer)
  • pageSize: (integer)

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.ContentsStreams",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "内容集合",
  "properties": {
    "stream": {
      "description": "集合",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "contents-stream"
      }
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "总数-所有内容总条数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "totalStreamCount": {
      "description": "内容流总数-按场景",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    },
    "contentStrategy": {
      "description": "内容显示策略，0-全量，1-增量",
      "type" : "string",
      "enum" : ["0", "1"],
      "javaEnumNames" : ["ALL", "INCREMENT"]
    },
    "lastTime": {
      "description": "最后内容时间",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "totalHistoryContentCount": {
      "description": "历史内容总数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

  • Response
  • Security

    用户ID

  • refreshTime: (string)

    增量获取时间，获取此时间之后内容；若为空则全量获取

  • pageNo: (integer)
  • pageSize: (integer)

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/delegate/contents/papapa get

get

啪啪啪推荐

get /delegate/contents/papapa

啪啪啪推荐

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Contents",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "内容集合",
  "properties": {
    "contents": {
      "description": "集合",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "content"
      }
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "总数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 500

服务端异常

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",

        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",

        "required": false
    },
    "status": {

}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/products/{product_id}/comments get

get

商品的评论列表

get /products/{product_id}/comments

商品的评论列表

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • product_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "required": true,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.ProductComments",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "评论集合",
  "properties": {
    "comments": {
      "description": "集合",
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "product-comment"
      }
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "总数",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 500

服务端异常

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",

  "type": "object",

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/suppliers/{supplier_id}/allproducts get

get

全部品牌

get /suppliers/{supplier_id}/allproducts

全部品牌

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • supplier_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • count: (integer - default: 10)

    当前页所展示的数据个数

    Example:

    10
  • start: (integer - default: 1)

    开始页，默认从第一页开始

    Example:

    1
  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Products",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "商品列表",
  "properties": {
    "productsContent": {
      "description": "商品内容",
      "type": "object",
      "$ref": "content"
    },
    "totalCount": {
      "description": "数量",
      "type": "integer",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/orders

订单资源

/orders/{order_id}/express post

post

订单发货

post /orders/{order_id}/express

订单发货

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • order_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.OrderExpress",
  "type": "object",
  "description": "订单发货",
  "properties": {
    "orderId": {
      "description": "订单ID",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "channel": {
      "description": "渠道",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "channelCode": {
      "description": "渠道码",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "memberId":{
      "description": "会员ID",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "expressList": {
      "description": "快递单号",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "expressContractorName": {
      "description": "快递商家名称",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    },
    "expressContractorCode": {
      "description": "快递商家code",
      "type": "string",
      "required": false
    }
  }
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/orders/{order_id}/returnproductplatformconfirm post

post

订单退货平台确认

post /orders/{order_id}/returnproductplatformconfirm

订单退货平台确认

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • order_id: required (string)

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

Type: application/json

Schema:

    },

  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/scan

/scan/barcode get

条形码查商品信息

get

根据条形码查商品信息

get /scan/barcode

根据条形码查商品信息

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • code: (string)

HTTP status code 200

请求成功

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Content",

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用

/version

版本

/version/latest get

get

获取当前最新版本

get /version/latest

获取当前最新版本

Secured by oauth_2_0

系统支持 OAuth 2.0 来验证所有的APIs

  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • x-la-authorization: (string)

    使用 oauth2.0 的方式获取access_token

  • x-la-session: (string)

    当前用户的sessionId

  • x-la-format: required (one of json)

    系统响应的数据格式，目前只有JSON一种

  • x-la-app-key: required (string)

    系统分配给客户端的唯一标识

  • x-la-sign-method: required (one of MD5)

    系统参数签名方式

  • guid: required (string)

    用户ID

Query Parameters

  • sign: required (string)

    对参数进行签名后的值，用来防止参数被篡改

  • deviceType: (string)

    android or ios

  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

{
  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

HTTP status code 404

资源不存在或当前访问的资源对象不存在

Body

Type: application/json

  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",

HTTP status code 500

服务端异常

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "description": "错误，请求错误时返回",
  "required": false,
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-03/schema",
  "javaType" : "org.nextspace.platform.api.gateway.model.Error",
  "type": "object",
  "properties" :{
    "errorCode" : {
        "description": "错误码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "message": {
        "description": "错误信息",
        "type": "string",
        "required": false
    },
    "status": {
        "description": "状态码",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    },
    "timestamp": {
        "description": "时间戳",
        "type": "integer",
        "required": false
    }
  }
}

Example:

{
  "errorCode": 0,
  "message": "Invalid access token.",
  "status": 401,
  "timestamp": 1378122137646
}

Secured by oauth_2_0

Headers

  • Authorization: (string)

    通常发送一个有效的OAuth 2的access token.不要和queryParameters里的access_token同时使用

HTTP status code 401

错误或过期的token. 如果用户或Dropbox撤销或过期了访问令牌，就会发生这种情况。要解决此问题，您应该重新验证用户

HTTP status code 403

错误的OAuth请求 (wrong consumer key, bad nonce, expired timestamp...). 不幸的是，重新验证用户也不会起作用
